#EQUATIONS

//Pontus HOM chemistry with alpha-pinene and limonene including aerosol phase

{1.}      APINOOA = R_HOM_O4 + OH :                   KDEC*0.10 ;
{2.}      LIMOOA = R_HOM_O4 + OH :                    KDEC*0.30 ;
{3.}      APINOOA = C107O2 + OH :                     KDEC*0.55*0.90 ;
{4.}      APINOOA = C109O2 + OH :                     KDEC*0.45*0.90 ;
{5.}      LIMOOA = LIMALAO2 + OH :                    KDEC*0.5*0.7 ;
{6.}      LIMOOA = LIMALBO2 + OH :                    KDEC*0.5*0.7 ;

// Add HOM formation from OH oxidation followed by autoxidation of MT:
// Berndt et al., 2016 gives lower estimated molar yield of RO2 (O:C=0.7) of 2.4 % for a-pinene, 0.9 % for B-pinene

{7.}      APINENE + OH = R_HOM_OH_O5 :                         0.025*1.3E-11*EXP(440/TEMP);
{8.}      BPINENE + OH = R_HOM_OH_O5 :                         0.01*2.38E-11*EXP(357/TEMP);
{9.}      LIMONENE + OH = R_HOM_OH_O5 :                        0.01*4.28D-11*EXP(401/TEMP);
{10.}     CARENE + OH = R_HOM_OH_O5 :                          0.025*1.60D-11*EXP(500./TEMP);

// AUTOXIDATION REACTIONS H-shifts + O2 addition:
{11.}     R_HOM_O4 = R_HOM_O6 :                   1.2D17*exp(-1.2077D4/TEMP); // 0.1*EXP(0./TEMP) ;
{12.}     R_HOM_O5 = R_HOM_O7 :                   1.2D18*exp(-1.2077D4/TEMP); // 0.1*EXP(0./TEMP) ;
{13.}     R_HOM_O6 = R_HOM_O8 :                   1.2D18*exp(-1.2077D4/TEMP); // 1.0*EXP(0./TEMP) ;
{14.}     R_HOM_O7 = R_HOM_O9 :                   6D17*exp(-1.2077D4/TEMP); // 0.1*EXP(0./TEMP) ;
{15.}     R_HOM_O8 = R_HOM_O10 :                  2D17*exp(-1.2077D4/TEMP); // 0.1*EXP(0./TEMP) ;
{16.}     R_HOM_O9 = R_HOM_O11 :                  1.2D17*exp(-1.2077D4/TEMP); // 0.05*EXP(0./TEMP) ;
{17.}     R_HOM_O10 = R_HOM_O12 :                 1.2D17*exp(-1.2077D4/TEMP); // 0.05*EXP(0./TEMP) ;
{18.}     R_HOM_O11 = R_HOM_O13 :                 1.2D16*exp(-1.2077D4/TEMP); // 0.01*EXP(0./TEMP) ;
{19.}     R_HOM_O12 = R_HOM_O14 :                 0.0*EXP(0./TEMP) ;

// Conversion of HOM alkoxy radicals to peroxy radicals (RO + O2 -> RO2)
{20.}     RHOM_O3 = R_HOM_O5 :                          KDEC*EXP(0./TEMP) ;
{21.}     RHOM_O4 = R_HOM_O6 :                          KDEC*EXP(0./TEMP) ;
{22.}     RHOM_O5 = R_HOM_O7 :                          KDEC*EXP(0./TEMP) ;
{23.}     RHOM_O6 = R_HOM_O8 :                          KDEC*EXP(0./TEMP) ;
{24.}     RHOM_O7 = R_HOM_O9 :                          KDEC*EXP(0./TEMP) ;
{25.}     RHOM_O8 = R_HOM_O10 :                         KDEC*EXP(0./TEMP) ;
{26.}     RHOM_O9 = R_HOM_O11 :                         KDEC*EXP(0./TEMP) ;
{27.}     RHOM_O10 = R_HOM_O12 :                        KDEC*EXP(0./TEMP) ;
{28.}     RHOM_O11 = R_HOM_O13 :                        KDEC*EXP(0./TEMP) ;
{29.}     RHOM_O12 = R_HOM_O14 :                        KDEC*EXP(0./TEMP) ;

//Functionalization of HOM RO2 when they react with NO (RO2 + NO -> RO + NO2)
{30.}     R_HOM_O4 + NO = RHOM_O3 + NO2 :             KRO2NO*1.0*EXP(0./TEMP) ;
{31.}     R_HOM_O5 + NO = RHOM_O4 + NO2 :             KRO2NO*1.0*EXP(0./TEMP) ;
{32.}     R_HOM_O6 + NO = RHOM_O5 + NO2 :             KRO2NO*1.0*EXP(0./TEMP) ;
{33.}     R_HOM_O7 + NO = RHOM_O6 + NO2 :             KRO2NO*0.9*EXP(0./TEMP) ;
{34.}     R_HOM_O8 + NO = RHOM_O7 + NO2 :             KRO2NO*0.85*EXP(0./TEMP) ;
{35.}     R_HOM_O9 + NO = RHOM_O8 + NO2 :             KRO2NO*0.8*EXP(0./TEMP) ;
{36.}     R_HOM_O10 + NO = RHOM_O9 + NO2 :            KRO2NO*0.6*EXP(0./TEMP) ;
{37.}     R_HOM_O11 + NO = RHOM_O10 + NO2 :           KRO2NO*0.5*EXP(0./TEMP) ;
{38.}     R_HOM_O12 + NO = RHOM_O11 + NO2 :           KRO2NO*0.3*EXP(0./TEMP) ;
{39.}     R_HOM_O13 + NO = RHOM_O12 + NO2 :           KRO2NO*0.0*EXP(0./TEMP) ;
{40.}     R_HOM_O14 + NO = RHOM_O13 + NO2 :           KRO2NO*0.0*EXP(0./TEMP) ;

//Fragmentation of HOM RO2 when they react with NO:
{41.}     R_HOM_O4 + NO = C717O2 + CH3COCH3 + NO2 :     0.4*KRO2NO*0.0*EXP(0./TEMP) ;
{42.}     R_HOM_O5 + NO = C717O2 + CH3COCH3+NO2 :       0.4*KRO2NO*0.0*EXP(0./TEMP) ;
{43.}     R_HOM_O6 + NO = C717O2 + CH3COCH3 + NO2 :     0.4*KRO2NO*0.0*EXP(0./TEMP) ;
{44.}     R_HOM_O7 + NO = C717O2 + CH3COCH3+NO2 :       0.4*KRO2NO*0.1*EXP(0./TEMP) ;
{45.}     R_HOM_O8 + NO = C717O2 + CH3COCH3 + NO2 :     0.4*KRO2NO*0.15*EXP(0./TEMP) ;
{46.}     R_HOM_O9 + NO = C717O2 + CH3COCH3+NO2 :       0.4*KRO2NO*0.2*EXP(0./TEMP) ;
{47.}     R_HOM_O10 + NO = C717O2 + CH3COCH3 + NO2 :    0.4*KRO2NO*0.4*EXP(0./TEMP) ;
{48.}     R_HOM_O11 + NO = C717O2 + CH3COCH3+NO2 :      0.4*KRO2NO*0.5*EXP(0./TEMP) ;
{49.}     R_HOM_O12 + NO = C717O2 + CH3COCH3 + NO2 :    0.4*KRO2NO*0.7*EXP(0./TEMP) ;
{50.}     R_HOM_O13 + NO = C717O2 + CH3COCH3+NO2 :      0.4*KRO2NO*1.0*EXP(0./TEMP) ;
{51.}     R_HOM_O14 + NO = C717O2 + CH3COCH3+NO2 :      0.4*KRO2NO*1.0*EXP(0./TEMP) ;

// RO2 + NO -> R=O + NO2 + HO2
{52.}     R_HOM_O4 + NO = HOM_O3CBN + NO2 + HO2 :           0.6*KRO2NO*0.0*EXP(0./TEMP) ;
{53.}     R_HOM_O5 + NO = HOM_O4CBN + NO2 + HO2 :           0.6*KRO2NO*0.0*EXP(0./TEMP) ;
{54.}     R_HOM_O6 + NO = HOM_O5CBN + NO2 + HO2 :           0.6*KRO2NO*0.0*EXP(0./TEMP) ;

// AUTOXIDATION REACTIONS H-shifts + O2 addition reaction proposed by Kurtn et al., 2015:
{1152.}     C107O2 = RHOM_O3 :                              9.20D-14*RO2*0.1 ;

// OH + MT autoxidation (Berndt et al., 2016):
{1155.}     R_HOM_OH_O5 = R_HOM_OH_O7 :                      2D17*exp(-1.2077D4/TEMP); // 0.3*EXP(0./TEMP) ;
{1156.}     R_HOM_OH_O6 = R_HOM_OH_O8 :                      6D16*exp(-1.2077D4/TEMP); // 0.05*EXP(0./TEMP) ;

{1158.}     R_HOM_OH_O8 = R_HOM_OH_O10 :                     3D16*exp(-1.2077D4/TEMP); // 0.02*EXP(0./TEMP) ;

// Conversion of HOM alkoxy radicals to peroxy radicals (RO + O2 -> RO2)
